### [184] [Wiener Hopf Analysis of Transient Mode-I/Mode-II Fracture in Rotating Heterogeneous Magnetoelastic Orthotropic Media under Initial Stresses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.15870)
*Diksha,Soniya Chaudhary,Pawan Kumar Sharma*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 研究了旋转、空间梯度磁弹性斜晶带中半无限裂纹在I型和II型加载条件下的断裂行为，并分析了梯度材料、旋转、磁弹性和初始应力等因素的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旋转、空间梯度磁弹性斜晶带中半无限裂纹在开裂（I型）和平面滑动（II型）条件下的断裂行为，以及初始法向应力。

Method: 通过空间域傅里叶变换和时间域拉普拉斯变换将控制场方程简化为可解析处理的形式。利用维纳-霍普夫方法求解边界值问题，得到应力强度因子（SIFs）的解析表达式，并通过广义切比雪夫-拉盖尔多项式方法进行拉普拉斯反演。

Result: 研究结果表明，梯度功能化显著影响SIFs的大小和时间演变，旋转具有稳定的作用，而磁弹性则产生依赖于模式的影响。

Conclusion: 该研究为先进的磁弹性复合材料在高性能旋转结构中的断裂行为提供了有价值的见解，适用于表面声波器件、飞机机翼和直升机旋翼等。

Abstract: This study investigates the fracture behavior under both opening (Mode I) and
in-plane sliding (Mode II) conditions for a semi-infinite crack in a rotating,
spatially graded magnetoelastic orthotropic strip with combined horizontal and
vertical initial normal stresses. The strip is assumed infinite in extent, with
the crack aligned along its longitudinal axis and parallel to the rotation
axis. The governing field equations are reduced to an analytically tractable
form by employing the Fourier transform in the spatial domain and the Laplace
transform in the temporal domain. The effect of a sudden application of
traction, represented by a Heaviside step function, is analyzed for both normal
and shear loading conditions. The resulting boundary-value problem is addressed
through the Wiener Hopf method, yielding analytical representations of the
stress intensity factors (SIFs). The near tip asymptotic stress fields are
evaluated to derive explicit SIF representations for each loading
configuration. Laplace inversion is performed using the generalized Chebyshev
Laguerre polynomial method. Numerical simulations are conducted for Uranium and
Graphite--Epoxy, with isotropic materials considered for comparison to assess
the role of anisotropy. The temporal evolution of the SIFs is investigated for
varying material gradation parameters, rotation rates, magnetoelastic coupling,
and initial stresses. Results reveal that functional grading significantly
influences both the magnitude and time evolution of the SIFs, rotation
introduces a stabilizing effect, and magnetoelasticity exhibits mode-dependent
impacts. These findings provide valuable insight into fracture behavior in
advanced magnetoelastic composites, with relevance to high-performance rotating
structures such as surface acoustic wave devices, aircraft wings, and
helicopter blades.

</details>


### [185] [High temporal stability of niobium superconducting resonators by surface passivation with organophosphonate self-assembled monolayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.15957)
*Harsh Gupta,Rui Pereira,Leon Koch,Niklas Bruckmoser,Moritz Singer,Benedikt Schoof,Manuel Kompatscher,Stefan Filipp,Marc Tornow*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: A new SAMs passivation method for Nb thin films effectively suppresses oxide regrowth, enhancing the stability of superconducting circuits and potentially enabling industrial-scale qubit fabrication.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Mitigating two level system (TLS) losses in superconducting circuits, a main limiting factor towards achieving high coherence times, requires controlling the formation of native oxides at the metal-air interface.

Method: Growth of alkyl-phosphonate self-assembled monolayers (SAMs) on Nb thin films following oxide removal. The impact of passivation was evaluated via the performance of coplanar waveguide resonators at 10mK, in terms of quality factor and resonant frequency, over six days of air exposure. A two-component TLS model was employed to discern distinct prominent loss channels for each resonator type.

Result: SAM-passivated resonators maintained excellent temporal stability, attributed to suppressed oxide regrowth, while un-passivated resonators exhibited an ~80% increase in loss at single-photon power levels. The characteristic TLS loss of the SAMs was quantified to be ~5x10^-7.

Conclusion: SAMs passivation methodology offers a promising route toward industrial-scale qubit fabrication, particularly where long-term device stability is critical.

Abstract: One main limiting factor towards achieving high coherence times in
superconducting circuits is two level system (TLS) losses. Mitigating such
losses requires controlling the formation of native oxides at the metal-air
interface. Here, we report the growth of alkyl-phosphonate self-assembled
monolayers (SAMs) on Nb thin films following oxide removal. The impact of
passivation was evaluated via the performance of coplanar waveguide resonators
at 10mK, in terms of quality factor and resonant frequency, over six days of
air exposure. Un-passivated resonators exhibited an ~80% increase in loss at
single-photon power levels, whereas SAM-passivated resonators maintained
excellent temporal stability, attributed to suppressed oxide regrowth. By
employing a two-component TLS model, we discern distinct prominent loss
channels for each resonator type and quantified the characteristic TLS loss of
the SAMs to be ~5x10^-7. We anticipate our passivation methodology to offer a
promising route toward industrial-scale qubit fabrication, particularly where
long-term device stability is critical.

</details>


### [186] [Modeling Energy- and Momentum-dependent Scattering Relaxation Times in a Semi-Classical Model of Charge Transport using the Self-Scattering Technique](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.15927)
*H. A. McDonough,Nicholas A. Mecholsky*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: "The self-scattering technique in Monte Carlo simulations can accurately recover energy- and momentum-dependent scattering relaxation times, contrary to initial assumptions. This technique, supported by theoretical analysis, improves charge transport simulation models, though certain relaxation time forms may cause implementation issues."


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: "Improvement of numerical methods for calculating charge transport quantities of materials from the Boltzmann transport equation (BTE) is important for prediction of material properties. Techniques that allow for more accurate models of scattering rates and band structures while remaining less computationally involved are valuable."

Method: "The self-scattering technique was analyzed and its ability to recover energy- and momentum-dependent scattering relaxation times in Monte Carlo simulations was demonstrated. The theory behind the technique was developed, showing that the probability distribution function of free-flight times created using the self-scattering algorithm matches the analytical expression generated by full relaxation times and probabilities. However, certain forms of relaxation times may cause the simulation to fail."

Result: "The relaxation times and the fraction of scattering type selected in the simulation matched the full rates implemented in the simulation, confirming that the self-scattering technique can recover energy- and momentum-dependent scattering relaxation times."

Conclusion: "Clarity about such techniques is important for improvement of charge transport simulation models and implementation of ab initio scattering rates and band structures."

Abstract: Improvement of numerical methods for calculating charge transport quantities
of materials from the Boltzmann transport equation (BTE) is important for
prediction of material properties. In particular, techniques which allow for
more accurate models of scattering rates and band structures while remaining
less computationally involved are valuable. The self-scattering technique is
one such technique for implementing energy- and momentum-dependent scattering
relaxation times in Monte Carlo simulations of charge transport or iterative
techniques for solving the BTE. While the technique initially uses a constant
relaxation time in the simulation algorithm, we found, upon analysis of the
technique, that the energy and momentum total scattering relaxation time may be
recovered. To show this, we preformed self-scattering Monte Carlo simulations
of electron transport for both energy-dependent and independent relaxation
times. The relaxation times and the fraction of scattering type selected in the
simulation matched the full rates implemented in the simulation. In order to
understand these results, we developed the theory behind the technique,
demonstrating that the probability distribution function of free-flight times
created using the self-scattering algorithm produces the analytical probability
distribution function expression generated by full energy, momentum and time
dependent relaxation times and probabilities. However, certain forms of
relaxation times may cause the simulation to fail, depending on implementation.
Clarity about such techniques is important for improvement of charge transport
simulation models and implementation of ab initio scattering rates and band
structures.

</details>


### [187] [Hybrid Monte Carlo Metadynamics (hybridMC-MetaD)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.15942)
*Charlotte Shiqi Zhao,Sun-Ting Tsai,Sharon C. Glotzer*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 提出 hybridMC-MetaD 算法，结合混合蒙特卡洛和调温元动力学，能处理非可微变量，加速罕见事件模拟，降低元动力学使用门槛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了增强元动力学的灵活性和适用性，允许使用更广泛的集体变量（CVs），特别是那些非可微的CVs。

Method: 结合了混合蒙特卡洛（hybridMC）算法和调温元动力学（Well-Tempered Metadynamics），提出了一种新的算法 hybridMC-MetaD，能够处理非可微的集体变量（CVs）。

Result: 通过五个罕见事件的分子动力学（MD）模拟案例（模型势能系统、氩系统冷凝、近硬球系统结晶、近硬双锥系统结晶和胶体悬浮液），成功演示了 hybridMC-MetaD 的用法。该算法能够沿着非可微 CVs 偏倚转换，显著加速了相变过程，并计算了自由能垒。首次报道了近硬双锥系统的自由能面，该系统的结晶主要由熵驱动。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的 hybridMC-MetaD 算法降低了元动力学的使用复杂度并提高了其可及性，有望激发对元动力学更大的兴趣和更广泛的应用。

Abstract: We propose the powerful integration of the Hybrid Monte Carlo (hybridMC)
algorithm and Well-Tempered Metadynamics. This new algorithm, hybridMC-MetaD,
enhances the flexibility and applicability of metadynamics by allowing for the
utilization of a wider range of collective variables (CVs), namely
non-differentiable CVs. We demonstrate the usage of hybridMC-MetaD through five
examples of rare events in molecular dynamics (MD) simulations, including a
rare transition in a model potential system, condensation of the argon system,
crystallization in a nearly-hard sphere system, a nearly-hard bipyramid system
and a colloidal suspension. By taking advantage of hybridMC, which combines
molecular dynamics (MD) and MC, we are able to bias the transitions along
non-differentiable CVs for all five cases, which would be unfeasible with
conventional MD simulations. Enabled by metadynamics, we observed significant
acceleration of the phase transitions and calculated free energy barriers using
the hybridMC-MetaD simulation data. For the nearly-hard bipyramid system whose
crystallization is primarily driven by entropy, we report the free energy
surface for the first time. Through our case studies, we show that our
hybridMC-MetaD scheme reduces the complexity of using metadynamics and
increases its accessibility. We believe the hybridMC-MetaD algorithm will
stimulate greater interest in, and foster broader applications of metadynamics.

</details>


### [188] [First-principles many-body study for electronic, optical, and excitonic properties of RbTlCl3 perovskite for solar cells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16264)
*Siddharth,Vinod Kumar Solet,Sudhir K. Pandey*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: RbTlCl$_{3}$ 钙钛矿在光伏应用中表现出强大的激子效应和高达 15.5% 的太阳能转换效率潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了探索具有高效率的光伏（PV）应用潜力的新型钙钛矿化合物，本文对 RbTlCl$_{3}$ 进行了详细的理论研究。

Method: 本文采用密度泛函理论（DFT）和多体激发态计算，结合自旋-轨道耦合（SOC）效应，详细研究了 RbTlCl$_{3}$ 的电子和光学性质。计算方法包括 PBE 和 PBEsol 泛函、独立粒子近似（IPA）、带隙修正的 IPA（IQPA）、考虑局域场效应（LFEs）的随机相位近似（RPA），以及 Bethe-Salpeter 方程（BSE）。

Result: 研究发现 RbTlCl$_{3}$ 的带隙为 0.89-0.95 eV。通过 BSE 计算，在 1.6 eV 处观察到 10.8 的介电函数虚部峰值，表明存在强烈的激子效应。四个主要束缚激子（bright excitons）的结合能为 299-350 meV，其在倒空间局域，在实空间离域。BSE 预测在 1.7 eV 处吸收系数最大为 3.6 $	imes$ $10^{6}$ cm$^{-1}$，反射率最低为 2.7%。在 0.5 $\mu$m 厚度下，估计的太阳能电池效率最高可达 15.5%。

Conclusion: RbTlCl$_{3}$ 是一种潜力巨大的单结薄膜太阳能电池材料，其显着的激子效应是吸收光谱的关键。

Abstract: We present a detailed many-body ab initio study of the valence-skipper
RbTlCl$_{3}$ perovskite compound for photovoltaic (PV) applications. The
electronic and optical properties, both with and without spin-orbit coupling,
have been calculated using density functional theory (DFT) and many-body
excited-state calculations. The band gap, which is indirect in nature, is found
to be 0.95 eV and 0.89 eV from PBE and PBEsol, respectively. The optical
properties have been computed using four different approximations: independent
particle approximation (IPA), IPA with scissor correction (IQPA), random phase
approximation for local-field effects (LFEs), and the Bethe-Salpeter equation
(BSE). The estimated highest value of the imaginary part of the dielectric
function using IQPA is 7 at 2 eV, which slightly decreases to 5.7 due to LFEs.
Within BSE, the peak value is obtained to be maximum at 1.6 eV with a magnitude
of 10.8, which indicates the strong excitonic effect below the optical gap.
Large number of bright and dark bound excitons are found, where the binding
energies of four main bound bright excitons are found in the range of 299-350
meV. The exciton amplitude in both reciprocal and real space is analyzed. The
main bound bright exciton is localized in the reciprocal space, while this
exhibits a delocalized nature in real space. The BSE predicts a highest
absorption coefficient of 3.6 $\times$ $10^{6}$ cm$^{-1}$ at 1.7 eV, while a
minimum reflectivity in the active region of the solar energy spectrum is
obtained to be around 2.7\%. Finally, the solar efficiency has been estimated
using the spectroscopic limited maximum efficiency approach and obtained
highest value is 15.5% at a thickness of 0.5 $\mu$m. These findings reveal a
significant excitonic effect in the absorption spectra of RbTlCl$_{3}$ and
highlight its potential as a promising material for single-junction thin-film
solar cells.

lack of training data for ML -- and in particular deep learning -- is a

identify the optimal measurement region with high precision. Thus, we establish

Abstract: The work function and cleavage energy of a surface are critical properties

semiconductor devices, and heterogeneous catalysis. While first principles
calculations are accurate in predicting these properties, their computational

screening approach with density functional theory (DFT) infeasible. Here, we
introduce FIRE-GNN (Force-Informed, Relaxed Equivariance Graph Neural Network),

breaking, and evaluate out-of-distribution generalization, demonstrating that

predictions. This model enables accurate and rapid predictions of the work
function and cleavage energy across a vast chemical space and facilitates the
discovery of materials with tuned surface properties

spin/lattice instabilities. Furthermore, potentially reflecting the competition

as low as 0.02 Wcm-1K-1. As a result, the thermoelectric figure of merit zT
reaches 0.22 at 460 K. These findings establish EuTe4 as a compelling platform
to explore novel types of thermoelectric materials with multiple electronic
instability.

Abstract: Strain engineering offers a powerful route to tailor topological electronic
structures in correlated oxides, yet conventional epitaxial strain approaches
introduce extrinsic factors such as substrate-induced phase transitions and
crystalline quality variations, which makes the unambiguous identification of
the intrinsic strain effects challenging. Here, we develop a flexural strain
platform based on van der Waals epitaxy and flexible micro-fabrication,

### [196] [Do 1-dimensional metals prefer to form even-numbered van der Waals clusters ?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16214)
*Subhojit Pal,John F. Dobson*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 平行金属链之间的范德华相互作用可能比简单成对相互作用更复杂，奇数链束可能比偶数链束更稳定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究平行准一维金属（如纳米管刷、纳米线阵列和生物结构）中的多链束范德华相互作用，特别是奇数组合（三链束、五链束等）的排斥性相互作用，以及这些相互作用对链束形成的影响。

Method: 非微扰范德华能量分析

Result: 研究发现，在某些情况下，奇数组合（如三个双链束）比偶数组合（如两个三链束）具有更负的范德华能量，表明奇数组合可能更稳定，这与之前的推测相反。

Conclusion: 该研究通过非微扰范德华能量分析，反驳了奇数组合（如三链束）比偶数组合（如双链束）更稳定的观点，并提出了奇数组合可能更稳定的反例。研究还探讨了六链束的范德华相互作用，以及除两两相互作用外的其他相互作用的相对贡献。

Abstract: Parallel quasi-one-dimensional metals are known to experience strong
dispersion (van der Waals, vdW) interactions that fall off unusually slowly
with separation between the metals. Examples include nanotube brushes,
nano-wire arrays, and also common biological structures. In a many-stranded
bundle, there are potentially strong multi-strand vdW interactions that go
beyond a simple sum of negative (attractive) pairwise inter-strand energies.
Perturbative analysis showed that these contributions alternate in sign, with
the odd (triplet, quintuplet, ...) terms being positive (repulsive). The
triplet case leds to the intriguing speculation that these strands may prefer
to coalesce into even-numbered bundles, which could have implications for the
formation kinetics of DNA, for example. Here we use a non-perturbative vdW
energy analysis to show that this conjecture is not true in general. As our
counter-example we consider 6 strands and show that 2 well-separated bundles of
3 strands have a more negative total vdW energy than 3 well-separated bundles
of 2 strands ( i.e. an odd-number preference). We also discuss a bundle of 6
strands and explore the relative contributions beyond pairwise interactions.

MnAl-Ga, MnAl-As) interfaces are considered. The interfacial geometries

adhesion energies compared to those terminated with Mn-, Al-, or MnAl-atomic
terminations. This indicates their greater interfacial stability. In contrast,
MnAl-, Mn-, or Al-terminated interfaces preserve near half-metallicity, whereas
Co- and CoCo-terminated geometries display a strongly metallic character. All
studied interfaces show enhanced magnetic moments relative to their bulk
counterparts, primarily arising from interfacial atoms and their nearest
neighbours. These findings offer valuable insights for optimizing Co2MnAl-based
heterostructures in spintronic applications.

### [199] [Symmetries in zero and finite center-of-mass momenta excitons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16409)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了对激子进行对称分类，并降低计算成本。

Method: 提出一个基于时间反转和空间群对称性的对称性框架，用于分析激子态。利用对称性获得整个布里渊区中对称相关准动量下的激子本征态，并根据对称性对激子进行分类。通过使用投影算符构建电子-空穴乘积态的对称性适配线性组合，对 BSE 哈密顿量进行分块对角化，从而实现激子态的透明组织，并直接获得其简并度、选择规则和对称性保护特征。

Result: 该框架能够对激子进行对称分类，并提供对它们的简并度、选择规则和对称性保护特征的直接访问。对单层 MoS2 的应用表明，激子不可约表示的分类和 BSE 哈密顿量的分块结构与群论推导的相容关系非常吻合。

Abstract: We present a symmetry-based framework for the analysis of excitonic states,
incorporating both time-reversal and space-group symmetries. We demonstrate the
use of time-reversal and space-group symmetries to obtain exciton eigenstates
at symmetry-related center-of-mass momenta in the entire Brillouin zone from
eigenstates calculated for center-of-mass momenta in the irreducible Brillouin
zone. Furthermore, by explicitly calculating the irreducible representations of
the little groups, we classify excitons according to their symmetry properties
across the Brillouin zone. Using projection operators, we construct
symmetry-adapted linear combinations of electron-hole product states, which
block-diagonalize the Bethe-Salpeter Equation (BSE) Hamiltonian at both zero
and finite exciton center-of-mass momenta. This enables a transparent
organization of excitonic states and provides direct access to their
degeneracies, selection rules, and symmetry-protected features. As a
demonstration, we apply this formalism to monolayer MoS$_{2}$, where the
classification of excitonic irreducible representations and the block structure
of the BSE Hamiltonian show excellent agreement with compatibility relations
derived from group theory. Beyond this material-specific example, the framework
offers a general and conceptually rigorous approach to the symmetry
classification of excitons, enabling significant reductions in computational
cost for optical spectra, exciton-phonon interactions, and excitonic band
structure calculations across a wide range of materials.

### [200] [Getting the manifold right: The crucial role of orbital resolution in DFT+U for mixed d-f electron compounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16435)
*Kinga Warda,Eric Macke,Iurii Timrov,Lucio Colombi Ciacchi,Piotr M. Kowalski*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Accurately modeling compounds with partially filled $d$ and $f$ shells is a challenge for density-functional theory due to self-interaction errors. Standard Hubbard $U$ corrections can mitigate these errors but often fail for hybridized states, leading to incorrect predictions.

Method: Careful disentanglement of localized and delocalized states, involving minimization of the mismatch between the spatial extension of projector functions and the true coordination geometry. This requires Wannier-like alternatives to atomic-orbital projector functions or corrections of Hubbard manifolds exclusively comprised of the most localized A-3d, U-5f and O-2p orbitals.

Result: Accurate predictions of electronic states and structural distortions in ternary monouranates (AUO$_4$, where A = Mn, Co, or Ni) were achieved, where standard $U$ corrections generally fail.

Conclusion: The proposed method accurately predicts electronic states and structural distortions in ternary monouranates, overcoming limitations of standard Hubbard U corrections. This approach is crucial for the computational prediction of fundamental properties of technologically important actinide solids.

Abstract: Accurately modeling compounds with partially filled $d$ and $f$ shells
remains a hard challenge for density-functional theory, due to large
self-interaction errors stemming from local or semi-local exchange-correlation
functionals. Hubbard $U$ corrections can mitigate such errors, but are often
detrimental to the description of hybridized states, leading to spurious force
contributions and wrong lattice structures. Here, we show that careful
disentanglement of localized and delocalized states leads to accurate
predictions of electronic states and structural distortions in ternary
monouranates (AUO$_4$, where A represents Mn, Co, or Ni), for which standard
$U$ corrections generally fail. Crucial to achieving such accuracy is a
minimization of the mismatch between the spatial extension of the projector
functions and the true coordination geometry. This requires Wannier-like
alternatives to atomic-orbital projector functions, or corrections of Hubbard
manifolds exclusively comprised of the most localized A-$3d$, U-$5f$ and O-$2p$
orbitals. These findings open up the computational prediction of fundamental
properties of actinide solids of critical technological importance.

### [201] [Phonon studies of the phase transition sequence in antiferroelectric single crystal of Pb(Hf0.83Sn0.17)O3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16472)
*Anirudh K. R.,Cosme Milesi-Brault,Christelle Kadlec,Dmitry Nuzhnyy,Andrzej Majchrowski,Magdalena Krupska-Klimczak,Irena Jankowska-Sumara,Elena Buixaderas*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: PbHf0.83Sn0.17O3经历三个相变，依次为中间相（IM）、反铁电相（AFE2）和反铁电相（AFE1）。Pb原子动力学随温度变化，并影响相变。立方相到AFE2相的转变路径经过IM相，可能由布里渊区中心的金失效驱动，并与反铁电畸变失相耦合。最终的AFE1相变是由布里渊区中心外的模式和晶胞的加倍驱动的。

Conclusion: 该研究通过THz、远红外和拉曼光谱研究了PbHf0.83Sn0.17O3的相变序列， Pb原子对其所有相变都敏感，并且其动力学随温度变化。随着温度降低，晶体经历了三个相变：首先是中间相（IM），其中THz和IR光谱在100 cm-1以下检测到极性声子，这对介电常数最大值和声子软化很重要。拉曼光谱检测到额外的非极性Pb原子涨落和软化。在较低温度下，通过非极性软模（反极性和反铁畸变）以及极性声子介电强度的重要下降，揭示了到反铁电相（AFE2）的另一个转变。最终相变到反铁电相（AFE1）是通过新模式的出现以及反极性位移增大时软模式频率的突然变化而揭示的。通过对称性分析和光学观测研究了畴形貌随温度的变化，识别了立方相到AFE2相的转变路径，该路径经过IM相（可能具有四方对称性），并由布里渊区中心的金失效驱动。该机制与反铁电畸变失相耦合，最终将材料驱动到AFE2相。最终相变到AFE1相是由布里渊区中心外的模式以及晶胞的进一步加倍自然产生的。

Abstract: The sequence of phase transitions in PbHf0.83Sn0.17O3 has been studied by
THz, far infrared and Raman spectroscopies, revealing the complementary
behaviour of both, polar and non-polar phonons and their impact on the
transition lattice dynamics. Pb atom is sensitive to all phase transitions,
changing its dynamics with temperature. As temperature decreases, the crystal
undergoes a sequence of three phase transitions. The first one to an
intermediate (IM) phase, in which polar fluctuations are detected by THz and IR
spectroscopy at frequencies below 100 cm-1 contributing to the maximum of
permittivity and revealing important softening. Additional antipolar Pb
fluctuations and softening were detected by Raman spectroscopy. At lower
temperature, another transition to an antiferroelectric (AFE2) phase is
revealed by nonpolar soft modes (antipolar and antiferrodistortive ones), and
by an important drop of the dielectric strength of polar phonons. The final
transition to the antiferroelectric phase (AFE1) is revealed by the appearance
of new modes and a sudden change in the frequency of the soft modes when the
antipolar shifts become larger. Using symmetry analysis and optical observation
to study how the domain pattern changes with temperature, we identified a path
for the cubic-AFE2 transition throughout the IM phase, of plausible tetragonal
symmetry, driven by an instability from the center of the Brillouin zone. This
mechanism coexists with antiferrodistortive instabilities that eventually drive
the material into the AFE2 phase. The final phase transition to the AFE1 phase
naturally follows from a mode outside the center of the Brillouin zone and a
further doubling of the unit cell.

</details>


### [202] [Machine Learning Time Propagators for Time-Dependent Density Functional Theory Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16554)
*Karan Shah,Attila Cangi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 利用自回归神经算子加速 TDDFT 电子动力学模拟，精度高，速度快。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种基于实时的 TDDFT 和自回归神经算子作为电子密度时间传播器来加速电子动力学模拟的新方法。

Abstract: Time-dependent density functional theory (TDDFT) is a widely used method to

data, our model achieves superior accuracy and computational speed compared to
traditional numerical solvers. We demonstrate the effectiveness of our model on
a class of one-dimensional diatomic molecules under the influence of a range of
laser parameters. This method has potential in enabling real-time, on-the-fly
modeling of laser-irradiated molecules and materials with varying experimental

### [203] [Constructing Long Paths in Graph Streams](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16022)
*Christian Konrad,Chhaya Trehan*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了图流模型下的最长路径问题。对于无向图，提出了一种单通道近似算法，并给出了空间下界。对于有向图，证明了单通道近似的局限性，需要更大的空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机在于图流模型下的计算挑战，特别是在构建长路径方面。许多已知算法在扩展现有路径时需要一个完整的通道来添加一个边，这引发了一个基本问题：是否需要多个通道才能构建非平凡长度的路径，或者一个通道是否足够？为了回答这个问题，研究者们深入探讨了单通道流模型下的最长路径问题。

Method: 该研究通过设计半流算法和证明空间下界来研究图流模型下的最长路径问题。对于无向图，提出了一种在插入-删除模型下，能够高概率找到平均度 d 的 3/1 倍长度的路径的算法，并且通过调整参数可以实现 α-近似的最长路径，所需空间为 O(n^2/α)。对于有向图，证明了在插入-only模型下，获取 n^{1-o(1)}-近似的最长路径需要 Ω(n^2) 的空间。此外，还分别证明了在插入-only模型下，无向图的近似比不能是小的常数因子，以及在插入-删除模型下，无向图的 α-近似需要 Ω(n^2/α^3) 的空间。

Result: 研究结果包括：1. 对于无向图，在插入-only和插入-删除模型下，存在半流算法，能以高概率计算出长度至少为平均度 d/3 的路径。2. 这些算法还可以提供最长路径的 α-近似，所需空间为 O~(n^2/α)。3. 对于有向图，即使在插入-only模型下，也无法实现上述近似结果。4. 证明了在有向图的插入-only模型下，计算最长路径的 (n^{1-o(1)})-近似需要 Ω(n^2) 的空间。5. 证明了在无向图的插入-only模型下，半流空间不足以对最长路径进行小常数因子近似。6. 证明了在无向图的插入-删除模型下，计算最长路径的 α-近似需要 Ω(n^2/α^3) 的空间。

Conclusion: 该研究在图流模型下研究了最长路径问题，并针对无向图和有向图分别提出了算法和空间下界。对于无向图，在插入-删除模型下，半流算法可以在高概率下找到平均度 d 的 3/1 倍长度的路径，或者在空间为 O(n^2/α) 下得到 α-近似的最长路径。但对于有向图，即使在插入-only模型下，也无法实现接近 n 的近似比，需要 Ω(n^2) 的空间。此外，研究还表明，在插入-only模型下，对于无向图，半流空间不足以获得小常数因子近似的最长路径；而在插入-删除模型下，获得 α-近似的最长路径需要 Ω(n^2/α^3) 的空间。

Abstract: In the graph stream model of computation, an algorithm processes the edges of
an input graph in one or more sequential passes while using a memory sublinear
in the input size. This model poses significant challenges for constructing
long paths. Many known algorithms tasked with extending an existing path as a
subroutine require an entire pass to add a single additional edge. This raises
a fundamental question: Are multiple passes inherently necessary to construct
paths of non-trivial lengths, or can a single pass suffice? To address this
question, we study the Longest Path problem in the one-pass streaming model. In
this problem, given a desired approximation factor $\alpha$, the objective is
to compute a path of length at least $\lp(G) / \alpha$, where $\lp(G)$ is the
length of a longest path in the input graph. We give algorithms as well as
space lower bounds for both undirected and directed graphs. Our results
include: We show that for undirected graphs, in both the insertion-only and the
insertion-deletion models, there are semi-streaming algorithms, that compute a
path of length at least $d /3$ with high probability, where $d$ is the average
degree of the graph. These algorithms can also yield an $\alpha$-approximation
to Longest Path using space $\tilde{O}(n^2 / \alpha)$. Next, we show that such
a result cannot be achieved for directed graphs, even in the insertion-only
model. We show that computing a $(n^{1 - o(1)})$-approximation to Longest Path
in directed graphs in the insertion-only model requires space $\Omega(n^2)$. We
further show two additional lower bounds. First, we show that semi-streaming
space is insufficient for small constant factor approximations to Longest Path
for undirected graphs in the insertion-only model. Last, in undirected graphs
in the insertion-deletion model, we show that computing an
$\alpha$-approximation requires space $\Omega(n^2 / \alpha^3)$.

</details>


### [204] [PIPQ: Strict Insert-Optimized Concurrent Priority Queue](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16023)
*Olivia Grimes,Ahmed Hassan,Panagiota Fatourou,Roberto Palmieri*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: PIPQ 是一种新的并发优先队列，通过优化插入操作的并行性来提高性能，尤其适用于插入密集型任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在设计一种严格且可线性化的并发优先队列，其设计重点在于实现插入操作的并行性，而非传统上加速删除最小元素的操作。

Method: PIPQ 采用双层结构：工作节点层和领导节点层。工作节点层提供每个线程的数据结构以实现快速并行插入。领导节点层包含优先队列中优先级最高的元素，从而可以处理删除最小元素的操作。

Result: 该方法的评估包括对不同数据访问模式、操作混合、运行时设置的探索，以及集成到基于图的应用程序中，结果表明 PIPQ 在各种情况下均优于现有解决方案。

Conclusion: PIPQ 在多种情况下，尤其是在插入占主导地位的工作负载中，表现优于竞争对手。

Abstract: This paper presents PIPQ, a strict and linearizable concurrent priority queue
whose design differs from existing solutions in literature because it focuses
on enabling parallelism of insert operations as opposed to accelerating
delete-min operations, as traditionally done. In a nutshell, PIPQ's structure
includes two levels: the worker level and the leader level. The worker level
provides per-thread data structures enabling fast and parallel insertions. The
leader level contains the highest priority elements in the priority queue and
can thus serve delete-min operations. Our evaluation, which includes an
exploration of different data access patterns, operation mixes, runtime
settings, and an integration into a graph-based application, shows that PIPQ
outperforms competitors in a variety of cases, especially with insert-dominant
workloads.

</details>

The first sentence of your response should be a concise summary of the paper's content. This summary should be in Chinese and no more than 16 characters long. For example, "Text analysis" or "Short paper".

Result: 给出了字符串中某个位置包含的MUS数量的$\
The first sentence of your response should be a concise summary of the paper's content. This summary should be in Chinese and no more than 16 characters long. For example, "Text analysis" or "Short paper".$界限。

Abstract: A string $w$ is said to be a minimal unique substring (MUS) of a string $T$
if $w$ occurs exactly once in $T$, and any proper substring of $w$ occurs at
least twice in $T$. It is known that the number of MUSs in a string $T$ of

present matching $\Theta(\sqrt{n})$ upper and lower bounds for the number
$|MUS(T,i)|$ of MUSs containing a position $i$ in a string $T$ of length $n$.

### [206] [Symmetry-breaking symmetry in directed spectral partitioning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16173)

Method: 通过打破经典谱双划分中的对称性来激励有向割边的对齐。

### [207] [Linear Layouts Revisited: Stacks, Queues, and Exact Algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16319)
*Thomas Depian,Simon D. Fink,Robert Ganian,Vaishali Surianarayanan*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 该研究提出了三种新算法，扩展了对栈和队列布局的理解：一是针对顶点完整性的固定参数算法，二是避免了双指数依赖的页宽度和页数参数算法，三是改进了 1 页队列布局的算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在解决栈和队列布局复杂性理论前沿的悬而未决的基本问题，并改进现有算法在参数化和依赖性方面的不足。

Method: （1）提出了一种针对顶点完整性参数的最小页栈和队列布局的固定参数算法，该算法利用了新开发的 Ramsey 剪枝技术。（2）提出了一种计算页宽度为 q 的 l 页栈和队列布局的 n^(O(q*l)) 算法，这是首次避免了参数双指数依赖的算法。（3）提出了一种计算 1 页队列布局的 2^(O(n)) 算法，该算法改进了之前的最快算法，并采用了与计算 2 页栈布局的子指数算法不同的技术。

Result: （1）为最小页栈和队列布局提供了一个关于顶点完整性的固定参数算法。（2）提供了一个避免双指数依赖的计算页宽度为 q 的 l 页栈和队列布局的算法。（3）提供了一个改进现有算法的 1 页队列布局的算法。

Conclusion: 该研究通过提供三种新算法，显著扩展了我们对计算栈和队列布局的理解，解决了现有算法参数化中的一些开放性问题。

Abstract: In spite of the extensive study of stack and queue layouts, many fundamental
questions remain open concerning the complexity-theoretic frontiers for
computing stack and queue layouts. A stack (resp. queue) layout places vertices
along a line and assigns edges to pages so that no two edges on the same page
are crossing (resp. nested). We provide three new algorithms which together
substantially expand our understanding of these problems:
  (1) A fixed-parameter algorithm for computing minimum-page stack and queue
layouts w.r.t. the vertex integrity of an n-vertex graph G. This result is
motivated by an open question in the literature and generalizes the previous
algorithms parameterizing by the vertex cover number of G. The proof relies on
a newly developed Ramsey pruning technique. Vertex integrity intuitively
measures the vertex deletion distance to a subgraph with only small connected
components.
  (2) An n^(O(q * l)) algorithm for computing l-page stack and queue layouts of
page width at most q. This is the first algorithm avoiding a double-exponential
dependency on the parameters. The page width of a layout measures the maximum
number of edges one needs to cross on any page to reach the outer face.
  (3) A 2^(O(n)) algorithm for computing 1-page queue layouts. This improves
upon the previously fastest n^(O(n)) algorithm and can be seen as a counterpart
to the recent subexponential algorithm for computing 2-page stack layouts
[ICALP'24], but relies on an entirely different technique.

</details>


### [208] [Going Beyond Twin-width? CSPs with Unbounded Domain and Few Variables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16389)
*Peter Jonsson,Victor Lagerkvist,Jorke M. de Vlas,Magnus Wahlström*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 该研究通过代数方法分析了具有无界域的约束满足问题（udCSP）的复杂性。研究发现，问题的复杂性取决于约束映射的类型（无限制、独热、单调）。特别是，对于单调映射，通过识别“连接符”多项式，确定了 FPT 边界，并将其与孪生素数宽度和投影网格秩联系起来，但非二元语言的 FPT 问题仍待解决。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机是解决具有少量变量但无界域的约束满足问题（udCSP），这在计算复杂性领域，特别是在参数化复杂性研究中，具有重要意义。近期关于 MinCSP 的 FPT 算法的研究，如布尔 MinCSP 和具有三个割请求的有向多割，都归约到 k 变量 udCSP，并且该领域的 W[1]-hard 构造也与 k 变量 udCSP 相关，这表明 udCSP 是理解这些问题参数化复杂性的关键。

Method: 该研究利用代数理论和伽罗瓦连接（基于偏多函数）来研究无界域约束满足问题（udCSP）的复杂性。具体来说，研究了三种类型的映射：无限制映射、独热映射和单调映射。对于单调映射，通过识别“连接符”多项式来分析其 FPT 边界，并将其与有界孪生素数宽度和有界投影网格秩联系起来。

Result: 对于无限制映射，udCSP 问题在几乎所有情况下都是 W[1]-hard 的。对于独热映射，udCSP 的复杂度特征与 Marx 对布尔加权 CSPs 的 FPT 偶发性结果相匹配。对于单调映射，研究发现“连接符”多项式是 FPT 边界。当“连接符”多项式缺失时，udCSP(Γ,Mo) 定义所有排列，问题为 W[1]-hard。当存在“连接符”多项式且语言为二元时，问题为 FPT，且与有界孪生素数宽度相关。对于非二元语言，虽然存在有界投影网格秩，但 FPT 问题仍未解决。 (Twin-Width IV; Bonnet et al., JACM 2024)

Conclusion: 所提出的 udCSP 框架通过将无界域约束表示为有限域基本语言中的一元映射集合，为研究其复杂性提供了一个代数理论。研究了三种映射类型：无限制、独热和单调。对于无限制映射，除平凡情况外，问题均为 W[1]-hard。对于独热映射，其复杂度特征与 Marx 对布尔加权 CSPs 的 FPT 偶发性结果一致。对于单调映射，我们表明其复杂度取决于我们称为有序多项式的受限标识符，其中“连接符”多项式被确定为可能的 FPT 边界。我们证明其缺失意味着 udCSP(Γ,Mo) 定义了所有排列，该问题为 W[1]-hard；而其存在对于二元语言意味着有界的孪生素数宽度，该问题为 FPT（孪生素数宽度 IV）。对于不适用孪生素数宽度的非二元语言，该多项式与有界投影网格秩的概念一致，但该情况下的 FPT 问题仍有待解决。

Abstract: We study a model of constraint satisfaction problems geared towards instances
with few variables but with domain of unbounded size (udCSP). Our model is
inspired by recent work on FPT algorithms for MinCSP where frequently both
upper and lower bounds on the parameterized complexity of a problem correspond
to $k$-variable udCSPs; e.g., the FPT algorithms for Boolean MinCSP (Kim et
al., SODA 2023) and Directed Multicut with three cut requests (Hatzel et al.,
SODA 2023) both reduce to k-variable udCSPs, and the canonical W[1]-hardness
construction in the area, Paired Min Cut by Marx and Razgon (IPL 2009), is
effectively a k-variable udCSP.
  The udCSP framework represents constraints with unbounded domains via a
collection $\mathcal{M}$ of unary maps into a finite-domain base language
$\Gamma$. We develop an algebraic theory for studying the complexity of
udCSP$(\Gamma,\mathcal{M})$ with a Galois connection based on partial
multifunctions.
  We study three types of maps: unrestricted, one-hot, and monotone. For
unrestricted maps, the problem is W[1]-hard for all but trivial cases, and for
one-hot maps, the characterization coincides with Marx' FPT dichotomy for
Boolean Weighted CSPs (Computational Complexity 2005). For the case of monotone
maps Mo, we show that the complexity depends on restricted identifies we call
ordered polymorphisms; we identify the "connector" polymorphism as the likely
FPT boundary. We show that its absence implies that udCSP($\Gamma$,Mo) defines
all permutations, and the problem is W[1]-hard; while its presence for a binary
language implies bounded twin-width, and the problem is FPT (Twin-Width IV;
Bonnet et al., JACM 2024). For non-binary languages, where twin-width does not
apply, the polymorphism coincides with a notion of bounded projected grid-rank;
however, we leave the FPT question for this case open.

</details>


### [209] [Quality control in sublinear time: a case study via random graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16531)
*Cassandra Marcussen,Ronitt Rubinfeld,Madhu Sudan*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 该研究提出了“质量控制问题”，旨在识别来自特定分布的高质量输入并拒绝低质量输入。研究发现，对于随机图和k-clique计数，此问题比单独测试分布或质量更有效率，查询和时间复杂度为p^{-O(k)}。该方法对于具有最大度Δ(H)的图样H，复杂度为p^{-O(Δ(H))}，显示了其在算法可靠性与效率方面的优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的主要动机是解决在实践中对算法输出结果的信任问题。许多算法在平均情况下的表现良好，但在面对特定输入时，其可靠性可能无法保证。因此，研究人员提出了“质量控制问题”，旨在设计能够区分来自特定分布（即高质量）的输入与非此分布（即低质量或对抗性生成）输入的算法。这种方法有望在保持可接受的准确性的同时，实现比单独测试数据分布或质量度量更优的效率。

Method: 研究人员首先定义了“质量控制问题”，并引入了一个“质量函数”ρ和一个数据分布D，目标是识别从D抽取的样本（即高质量样本）并拒绝其他样本。然后，他们将研究重点放在该问题的亚线性版本上，即查询和时间复杂度均优于输入大小N。作为案例研究，他们选择了随机图 G_{n,p} 和 k-clique 计数函数 ρ_k，并分析了在这些条件下质量控制问题的可解性。通过与现有算法（例如，测试 G_{n,p} 分布或测试 ρ_k(G) ≈ 1）的比较，他们量化了质量控制方法在效率上的优势，证明了其查询和时间复杂度远低于现有方法。

Result: 研究人员证明了在随机图 G_{n,p} 上，使用 k-clique 计数函数 ρ_k 作为质量函数时，质量控制问题可以在 p^{-O(k)} 的查询和时间复杂度内解决。这比单独测试 G_{n,p} 分布（即使只有一个样本也无法完成）或测试 ρ_k(G) ≈ 1（需要 p^{-\Omega(k^2)} 个样本）的效率要高得多。更普遍地说，对于具有最大度 Δ(H) 的任意图样 H，质量控制问题可以在 p^{-O(Δ(H))} 的查询和运行时间内解决，证明了质量控制在这些场景下比传统方法具有显著的效率优势。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一个名为“质量控制问题”的新算法问题类别，其目标是在从特定分布中抽取的样本具有高“质量”（由质量函数ρ衡量）的同时，拒绝质量较低的输入。研究特别关注了亚线性查询版本的质量控制问题，即在查询和时间复杂度上优于输入大小N。研究人员以随机图 G_{n,p} 和 k-clique 计数函数 ρ_k 为例进行了案例研究，并证明了与单独测试 G_{n,p} 分布或测试 ρ_k(G) ≈ 1 相比，质量控制问题在这种情况下可以更高效地解决，查询和时间复杂度为 p^{-O(k)}。更广泛地说，对于具有最大度 Δ(H) 的图样 H，相应的质量控制问题可以在 p^{-O(Δ(H))} 的查询和运行时间内解决，这表明质量控制在这些设置下具有多项式以上的效率优势。

Abstract: Many algorithms are designed to work well on average over inputs. When
running such an algorithm on an arbitrary input, we must ask: Can we trust the
algorithm on this input? We identify a new class of algorithmic problems
addressing this, which we call "Quality Control Problems." These problems are
specified by a (positive, real-valued) "quality function" $\rho$ and a
distribution $D$ such that, with high probability, a sample drawn from $D$ is
"high quality," meaning its $\rho$-value is near $1$. The goal is to accept
inputs $x \sim D$ and reject potentially adversarially generated inputs $x$
with $\rho(x)$ far from $1$. The objective of quality control is thus weaker
than either component problem: testing for "$\rho(x) \approx 1$" or testing if
$x \sim D$, and offers the possibility of more efficient algorithms.
  In this work, we consider the sublinear version of the quality control
problem, where $D \in \Delta(\{0,1\}^N)$ and the goal is to solve the $(D
,\rho)$-quality problem with $o(N)$ queries and time. As a case study, we
consider random graphs, i.e., $D = G_{n,p}$ (and $N = \binom{n}2$), and the
$k$-clique count function $\rho_k := C_k(G)/\mathbb{E}_{G' \sim
G_{n,p}}[C_k(G')]$, where $C_k(G)$ is the number of $k$-cliques in $G$. Testing
if $G \sim G_{n,p}$ with one sample, let alone with sublinear query access to
the sample, is of course impossible. Testing if $\rho_k(G)\approx 1$ requires
$p^{-\Omega(k^2)}$ samples. In contrast, we show that the quality control
problem for $G_{n,p}$ (with $n \geq p^{-ck}$ for some constant $c$) with
respect to $\rho_k$ can be tested with $p^{-O(k)}$ queries and time, showing
quality control is provably superpolynomially more efficient in this setting.
More generally, for a motif $H$ of maximum degree $\Delta(H)$, the respective
quality control problem can be solved with $p^{-O(\Delta(H))}$ queries and
running time.

</details>

### [210] [Dual Topology as a Fingerprint of Relativistic Altermagnetism in AgF$_2$ Monolayer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.15944)
*J. W. González,R. A. Gallardo,N. Vidal-Silva,A. M. León*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: AgF$_2$单层材料在铁弹性畸变下实现了电子和磁孤子的双重拓扑态，并在横向霍尔效应中具有清晰的实验指纹。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索未被充分研究的、能够统一不同准粒子的拓扑相，特别是在反演对称性破缺的磁异质材料中。

Method: 通过理论计算和分析，揭示了AgF$_2$单层材料在铁弹性畸变下如何打破反演对称性，并触发相对论自旋-轨道效应，进而同时赋予电子和磁孤子非平凡的拓扑特性。

Result: AgF$_2$单层材料在铁弹性畸变下表现出双重拓扑态，电子价带拥有相反的陈数($C^E=	ext{±}3$)，磁孤子能谱呈现出完整的拓扑能隙和手征能带($C^M=	ext{±}1$)。

Conclusion: AgF$_2$单层材料为研究由单一铁弹性畸变驱动的双重拓扑态提供了一个实际的材料平台，该平台实现了由电子和磁振子贡献的、具有相反陈数的拓扑相，并可在横向霍尔效应中清晰地体现出来。这为设计本征混合量子物种开辟了新方向。

Abstract: Altermagnets have emerged as a fertile ground for quantum phenomena, but
topological phases unifying different quasiparticles remain largely unexplored.
Here, we demonstrate that monolayer AgF$_2$ hosts a dual topological state,
driven by a single ferroelastic distortion. This polar transition breaks
inversion symmetry and unleashes relativistic spin-orbit effects,
simultaneously imparting non-trivial topology to electrons and magnons. The
result is valence bands with opposite Chern numbers, $C^E=\pm3$, and a magnon
spectrum with a full topological gap and chiral bands, $C^M=\pm1$. This work
realizes topological altermagnonics in a tangible material platform, with a
clear experimental fingerprint in the transverse thermal Hall effect. The
coexistence of fermionic and bosonic topology in AgF$_2$ opens new directions
for designing intrinsically hybrid quantum matter.

### [211] [Strong Correlation Driven Quadrupolar to Dipolar Exciton Transitions in a Trilayer Moiré Superlattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16009)
*Yuze Meng,Lei Ma,Li Yan,Ahmed Khalifa,Dongxue Chen,Shuai Zhang,Rounak Banerjee,Takashi Taniguchi,Kenji Watanabe,Seth Ariel Tongay,Benjamin Hunt,Shi-Zeng Lin,Wang Yao,Yong-Tao Cui,Shubhayu Chatterjee,Su-Fei Shi*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三层过渡金属二硫属化物莫尔超晶格中的额外层自由度支持了四极子激子等新颖激子物种的出现，这些物种展现出独特的激子相互作用，并有望实现有趣的激子相及其量子相变。同时，莫尔超晶格中存在的强电子关联（例如，莫特绝缘体和广义维格纳晶体的观察）为操纵这些新的激子态和由此产生的集体激子相提供了直接途径。

Method: 本研究通过调控三层过渡金属二硫属化物莫尔超晶格中的激子密度或静电掺杂，利用强激子-激子和电子-激子相互作用（源于鲁棒的电子关联），实现了四极子激子和偶极子激子之间的可控转变。

Result: 研究证实，强激子-激子和电子-激子相互作用能够被用来可控地驱动四极子激子和偶极子激子之间的转变。

Conclusion: 本研究通过调控三层过渡金属二硫属化物莫尔超晶格中的激子密度或静电掺杂，利用强激子-激子和电子-激子相互作用，成功实现了四极子激子和偶极子激子之间的可控转变。研究结果增进了对四极子激子的基本理解，并为探索和工程化半导体莫尔体系中的多体量子现象开辟了新途径。

Abstract: The additional layer degree of freedom in trilayer moir\'e superlattices of
transition metal dichalcogenides enables the emergence of novel excitonic
species, such as quadrupolar excitons, which exhibit unique excitonic
interactions and hold promise for realizing intriguing excitonic phases and
their quantum phase transitions. Concurrently, the presence of strong
electronic correlations in moir\'e superlattices, as exemplified by the
observations of Mott insulators and generalized Wigner crystals, offers a
direct route to manipulate these new excitonic states and resulting collective
excitonic phases. Here, we demonstrate that strong exciton-exciton and
electron-exciton interactions, both stemming from robust electron correlations,
can be harnessed to controllably drive transitions between quadrupolar and
dipolar excitons. This is achieved by tuning either the exciton density or
electrostatic doping in a trilayer semiconducting moir\'e superlattice. Our
findings not only advance the fundamental understanding of quadrupolar excitons
but also usher in new avenues for exploring and engineering many-body quantum
phenomena through novel correlated excitons in semiconducting moir\'e systems.

### [212] [Controlling resonant spin photocurrent using magnetic field; application to a magnetoelectric oxide Cr2O3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16028)
*Zhuo-Cheng Gu,Hiroaki Ishizuka*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 研究了Cr2O3的Magnon自旋光电流，发现线性和圆偏振波均可激发布Magnon自旋流，并讨论了磁场依赖性，为实验验证提供了方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Cr2O3材料中的Magnon自旋光电流。

Method: 使用非线性响应理论。

Result: 线性和圆偏振电磁波都可以通过单Magnon过程产生Magnon自旋流。线偏振波在没有静态磁场的情况下也能感生自旋流，而圆偏振波只有在存在静态磁场时才能感生自旋流，并且其方向会随着磁场反转而反转。外部磁场依赖性和对不同偏振的不同响应使得自旋光电流可以与自旋泵或其他效应区分开来，便于实验验证。

Conclusion: Cr2O3是一种有前途的实验性Magnon光电流研究材料。

Abstract: We study the magnon spin photocurrent in effective spin models for Cr2O3, a
material known for its magnetoelectric effect. Using nonlinear response theory,
we show that magnon spin current can be generated by both linearly and
circularly polarized electromagnetic waves via one-magnon processes. While
linearly polarized waves induce a spin current even in the absence of a static
magnetic field, circularly polarized waves lead to a spin current only when a
static field is present, and the current reverses its direction upon field
inversion. The distinct dependence on the external magnetic field and the
contrasting responses to different polarizations allow the spin photocurrent to
be differentiated from competing effects such as spin pumping or inhomogeneous
heating, facilitating experimental verification. These results suggest that
Cr2O3 is a promising candidate for experimental studies of magnon photocurrent.

</details>


### [213] [Ultrafast Laser-Induced Magnetic Relaxation in Artificial Spin Ice Driven by Dipolar Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16231)
*D. Pecchio,S. Sahoo,O. Chubykalo-Fesenko,S. Koraltan,G. M. Macauley,T. Thomson,D. Suess,V. Scagnoli,L. J. Heyderman*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 飞秒激光脉冲可以超快地控制人工自旋冰的磁状态，通过激光退火可实现高基态序，为自旋计算和存储开辟新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本研究利用飞秒激光脉冲激发，结合时间分辨磁光克尔效应测量和易位磁力显微镜，并辅以包含Landau-Lifshitz-Bloch动力学的能量势垒计算和微磁模拟，来研究和控制人工自旋冰的磁弛豫过程。

Result: 研究证明了飞秒激光脉冲可以诱导人工自旋冰的超快弛豫，并在居里温度以下的瞬态窗口中，通过偶极相互作用驱动集体磁排序，形成基态序的特征——扩展的I型顶点畴。此外，通过激光退火方案，可以将基态顶点占有率提高到92%以上。

Conclusion: 该研究通过飞秒激光脉冲激发，实现了对方波纹状人工自旋冰的磁弛豫的超快控制，并展示了通过定制的递减激光退火方案可以提高基态序，实现了超过92%的基态顶点占有率。这为在自旋计算和内存技术中实现人工自旋冰的超快和空间选择性磁态控制开辟了道路，并强调了热涨落、静磁耦合和瞬态磁化动力学之间的关键相互作用。

Abstract: It is of great interest to develop methods to rapidly and effectively control
the magnetic configurations in artificial spin ices, which are arrangements of
dipolar coupled nanomagnets that have a variety of fascinating collective
magnetic phenomena associated with them. This is not only valuable in terms of
acquiring fundamental understanding but is also important for future
high-performance applications. Here, we demonstrate ultrafast control of
magnetic relaxation in square artificial spin ice through femtosecond laser
pulsed excitation, enabling rapid access to low-energy states via dipolar
interactions. Time-resolved magneto-optical Kerr effect measurements reveal
that, after laser-induced demagnetization, the magnetization recovers within
picoseconds. During this brief transient window, dipolar coupling drives a
collective magnetic ordering. Ex-situ magnetic force microscopy confirms the
emergence of extended Type I vertex domains, characteristic of ground-state
ordering, thus establishing ultrafast laser-driven relaxation as a route to
attain the low-energy states. Through complementary energy barrier calculations
and micromagnetic simulations incorporating Landau-Lifshitz-Bloch dynamics, we
elucidate the underlying mechanism: transient ultrafast demagnetization
followed by rapid remagnetization that enables a dipolar-driven collective
rearrangement. Moreover, a tailored decreasing-fluence laser annealing protocol
is shown to enhance ground-state ordering, consistently achieving over 92%
ground-state vertex populations. This work opens the way to ultrafast and
spatially selective control of magnetic states in artificial spin ice for
spin-based computation and memory technologies, and highlights the critical
interplay of thermal fluctuations, magnetostatic coupling, and transient
magnetization dynamics.

### [214] [Magneto-conductivity and CME in Dirac semimetals from Keldysh technique in Landau levels basis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16266)
*Ruslan A. Abramchuk*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: This study uses advanced techniques to analyze magnetoconductivity in Dirac semimetals, offering insights into electron behavior and relaxation mechanisms, and validating findings against experimental results.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To study magnetoconductivity in Dirac semimetals, particularly in materials like ZrTe5 where negative magnetoresistance was observed, and to understand the underlying physics beyond the conventional chiral magnetic effect (CME) explanation.

Method: Using the Non-equilibrium Diagram Technique (NDT, or the Keldysh technique) applied to a semi-realistic model Hamiltonian for Dirac semimetals, this paper derives kinetic equations to investigate electron relaxation (due to phonons and disorder) and calculates the DC magnetoconductivity.

Result: The paper calculates the DC magnetoconductivity as a function of magnetic field strength and temperature and compares the temperature dependencies with available experimental data.

Conclusion: This paper derives kinetic equations using the Non-equilibrium Diagram Technique (NDT) to study magnetoconductivity in Dirac semimetals, considering electron relaxation due to phonons and disorder, and compares the results with experimental data for ZrTe5.

Abstract: Negative magnetoresistance in Dirac semimetals is conventionally considered
as a manifestation of chiral magnetic effect (CME), by means of a postulated
Chiral Kinetic equation. In this paper we study magnetoconductivity in large
Fermi energy Dirac semimetals, in one of which (ZrTe$_5$) the effect was
observed for the first time. Starting with a Hamiltonian for a semi-realistic
model of such a Dirac semimetal, we apply the Non-equilibrium Diagram Technique
(NDT, or the Keldysh technique) to derive the kinetic equations, to investigate
the electrons relaxation due to interaction with phonons and disorder, and,
finally, to calculate the DC magnetoconductivity (the longitudinal to magnetic
field component of conductivity) as a function of magnetic field strength and
temperature. Finally, we compare the obtained temperature dependencies with
available to us experimental data.

### [215] [Observation of negative orbital torque from Vanadium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16339)
*Nikhil Vijayan,Durgesh Kumar,Ao Du,Lei Gao,Zijie Xiao,Hai I. Wang,Rahul Gupta,Gerhard Jakob,Sachin Krishnia,Yuriy Mokrousov,Mathias Kläui*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: Vanadium exhibits a negative orbital Hall effect with high efficiency, showing potential for spintronic applications. Its torque efficiency depends on adjacent materials and increases with thickness, outperforming Platinum at higher thicknesses.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to systematically investigate the orbital torques generated from the light metal Vanadium (V) and to understand its properties, particularly the sign and efficiency of the orbital Hall effect (OHE). The researchers aimed to compare V with established materials like Pt and quantify its OHE characteristics, such as orbital Hall conductivity and diffusion length.

Method: The study presents systematic investigations of orbital torques in Vanadium (V). It involves fabricating heterostructures with ferromagnetic layers (Ni/V and FeCoB/V) and a reference layer (Pt). The damping-like torque (DLT) was measured and analyzed in relation to the electric field, ferromagnetic layer material, and V layer thickness. Fitting the experimental data using the drift-diffusion equation allowed for the extraction of effective orbital Hall conductivity and orbital diffusion length.

Result: The study revealed a negative orbital torque in V. The damping-like torque (DLT) per unit electric field was found to be approximately seven times more efficient in Ni/V compared to FeCoB/V. The sign of the DLT per unit electric field in V is opposite to that in Pt. The DLT per unit electric field increases with V layer thickness, maintaining its negative sign, and surpasses Pt's efficiency at higher V thicknesses. The extracted effective orbital Hall conductivity is $-(1.46 
eq 0.09)\,\frac{\hbar}{2e}\,\times 10^{5}\,\Omega^{-1}\,\mathrm{m}^{-1}$, and the orbital diffusion length is $(13.7 
eq 0.9)\,\mathrm{nm}$.

Conclusion: The study confirms the existence of a negative orbital Hall effect (OHE) in Vanadium (V), characterized by a negative orbital torque. The damping-like torque (DLT) efficiency in V depends on the adjacent ferromagnetic layer, showing significantly higher torque efficiency in Ni/V compared to FeCoB/V. The DLT in V exhibits an opposite sign to that in Platinum (Pt). The DLT per unit electric field increases with V layer thickness and remains negative across all thicknesses, exceeding Pt's efficiency at higher V thicknesses. The research extracts a high effective orbital Hall conductivity of $-(1.46 
eq 0.09)\,\frac{\hbar}{2e}\,\times 10^{5}\,\Omega^{-1}\,\mathrm{m}^{-1}$ and a long orbital diffusion length of $(13.7 
eq 0.9)\,\mathrm{nm}$ in V.

Abstract: We present systematic investigations of orbital torques generated from the
light metal $V$, revealing a negative orbital torque. We observe that the
damping-like torque (DLT) per unit electric field depends on the choice of the
ferromagnetic layer, with approximately seven times higher torque efficiency in
$Ni/V$ as compared to $Fe_{60}Co_{20}B_{20}/V$. We find the sign of DLT per
unit electric field from $V$ is opposite to that from $Pt$. These results
collectively confirm the existence of negative orbital Hall effect (OHE) in
$V$. Furthermore, the DLT per unit electric field increases with the $V$ layer
thickness, maintaining the negative sign at all thicknesses. We also note that
the DLT per unit electric field exceeds that of the $Pt$ reference samples at
higher $V$ thicknesses. Through fitting using the drift-diffusion equation, we
extract a high effective orbital Hall conductivity of $-(1.46 \pm
0.09)\,\frac{\hbar}{2e}\,\times 10^{5}\,\Omega^{-1}\,\mathrm{m}^{-1}$ and a
long orbital diffusion length of $(13.7 \pm 0.9)\,\mathrm{nm}$ in $V$. .

</details>


### [216] [Mechanical Reinforcement of Graphene via Wrinkling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16340)
*Hadi Arjmandi-Tash,Roshan Prasad,Hanqing Liu,Gerard Verbiest,Dominic Vella,Farbod Alijani*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 通过在石墨烯上制造皱纹，可以大大提高其刚度，从而制造出更坚固、更灵敏的纳米机械设备。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机械悬臂梁在纳米技术中至关重要，但在原子极限下，其低弯曲刚度带来的稳定性挑战限制了其应用。本研究旨在通过提高石墨烯悬臂梁的机械刚度和稳定性，克服这一挑战。

Method: 本研究提出了一种皱纹诱导硬化方法，通过在悬浮的单层石墨烯上引入皱纹，来提高其弯曲刚度。研究人员使用纳米压痕和共振测量技术，验证了该方法能够将石墨烯的弯曲刚度提高几个数量级，并观察到其在振动响应中的变化，证实了弯曲效应在单原子层中的重要性。

Result: 本研究成功制备了具有增强弯曲刚度的石墨烯悬臂梁，其弯曲刚度在 $10^6$ 和 $10^7$ eV 之间，同时保持了飞克量级的质量。实验证实，皱纹诱导硬化显著提高了石墨烯悬臂梁的平面内和平面外刚度，并影响了其振动响应。

Conclusion: 本研究通过引入皱纹诱导硬化方法，显著提高了单层石墨烯的弯曲刚度，实现了机械强度高且质量仅为飞克量级的石墨烯悬臂梁，这为纳米机械传感和悬臂梁技术开辟了新方向。

Abstract: Mechanical cantilevers are central to nanotechnology, with ultimate
sensitivity achieved at the atomic limit, where low bending rigidity makes
stability the fundamental challenge. Here, we introduce a wrinkle-induced
stiffening approach that enhances the bending rigidity of monolayer graphene by
several orders of magnitude, enabling the fabrication of mechanically robust
graphene cantilevers. When suspended over microcavities, these wrinkled
membranes exhibit significant increases in both in-plane and out-of-plane
stiffness, as confirmed by nanoindentation and resonance measurements, which
also reveal that enhanced bending rigidity strongly influences their
vibrational response. This behavior marks a transition from tension-dominated
mechanics to a regime where bending effects become prominent, even in a single
atomic layer. By sculpting these structures, we realize graphene cantilevers
with measured bending rigidities between $10^6$ and $10^7$ eV, while
maintaining femtogram-scale mass. These findings open new directions in
nanomechanical sensing and cantilever-based technologies.

</details>

### [217] [Observer-Free Sliding Mode Control via Structured Decomposition: a Smooth and Bounded Control Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.15787)
*Jaafar Gaber*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 提出了一种新的无观测器滑模控制方法，该方法通过显式结构补偿消除了对观测器的需求，减少了抖振，并提高了鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 消除对状态观测器和高阶导数的需求，减少抖振，并产生平滑、有界的控制信号。

Method: 提出了一种基于显式结构补偿的无观测器滑模控制（SMC）方法，通过分解 s = α - β。

Result: 仿真结果证实了其在噪声、干扰和参数变化下对基准非线性系统（单摆、范德波尔、杜芬、网络化系统）的鲁棒性和稳定性。基于李亚普诺夫的稳定性证明证实了收敛性。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了一种可扩展且实用的传统滑模控制（SMC）的替代方案，非常适合嵌入式和分布式环境。

Abstract: In this paper, we introduce an observer-free sliding mode control (SMC)
method based on explicit structural compensation via the decomposition \( s =
\alpha - \beta \). The proposed formulation eliminates the need for state
observers and higher-order derivatives, reduces chattering, and yields smooth,
bounded control signal. Simulation results confirms its robustness and
stability on benchmark nonlinear systems (pendulum, Van der Pol, Duffing, and
networked systems) under noise, disturbances, and parameter variations. A
Lyapunov-based stability proof confirms convergence. This method provides a
scalable and practical alternative to traditional SMC, well suited for embedded
and distributed environments.

### [218] [Konzepte zur Effizienzsteigerung von Traktionsmotoren in batterieelektrischen Fahrzeugen durch den Einsatz neuartiger teillastoptimierbarer Motor- und Invertertopologien](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.15869)
*Christoph Sachs,Martin Neuburger*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了提高未来电动汽车的效率，必须减少电池驱动汽车的传动系统损耗。

Result: 谐波电机损耗占标准 B6-2L 300 kW iPMSM 配置总 eDrive 损耗的 30% 以上。

Abstract: To increase the efficiency of future electric vehicles, it is crucial to
reduce drivetrain losses in battery-powered vehicles. This enables either an
increase in driving range or overall cost savings by reducing battery capacity
while maintaining the same range. Harmonic motor losses account for an
avoidable share of more than 30% of the total eDrive losses in standard B6-2L
300 kW iPMSM configurations. These losses result from high-frequency voltage
distortion across the motor windings, which can be reduced through various
approaches. Of great importance is the classification of cost-neutral and
low-cost concepts for loss reduction. The following presents and categorizes
approaches to loss reduction that have been developed by research and industry
in recent years. In particular, novel part-load-capable motor and inverter
concepts are introduced, which enable motor switching or multilevel operation
to reduce harmonic losses in the part-load range.

### [219] [Solving Three-phase AC Infeasibility Analysis to Near-zero Optimality Gap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.15937)
*Bikram Panthee,Amritanshu Pandey*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 通过将三相不可行性分析（TPIA）问题重新表述为非凸双线性规划（BLP）并使用空间分支定界（SBnB）算法，结合边界缩紧技术，可以更准确高效地解决大规模电网的升级问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原始三相不可行性分析（TPIA）问题是非凸的，可能存在局部最小值和鞍点，导致次优的电网升级。本研究旨在解决此问题。

Method: 将原始非凸非线性规划（NLP）重新表述为精确的非凸双线性规划（BLP），然后应用空间分支定界（SBnB）算法求解，并通过包含变量过滤和分解的边界缩紧算法来提高SBnB的性能。

Result: 所提出的方法可以解决大规模三相不可行性分析问题（>5k节点），最优性间隙小于10e-4，并将SBnB的运行时间缩短多达97%。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法能够以小于10e-4的最优性间隙解决大规模三相不可行性分析问题（超过5k个节点），并通过包含预解例程将SBnB的运行时间缩短多达97%。

Abstract: Recent works have shown the use of equivalent circuit-based infeasibility
analysis to identify weak locations in distribution power grids. For
three-phase power flow problems, when the power flow solver diverges,
three-phase infeasibility analysis (TPIA) can converge and identify weak
locations. The original TPIA problem is non-convex, and local minima and saddle
points are possible. This can result in grid upgrades that are sub-optimal. To
address this issue, we reformulate the original non-convex nonlinear program
(NLP) as an exact non-convex bilinear program (BLP). Subsequently, we apply the
spatial branch-and-bound (SBnB) algorithm to compute a solution with near-zero
optimality gap. To improve SBnB performance, we introduce a bound tightening
algorithm with variable filtering and decomposition, which tightens bounds on
bilinear variables. We demonstrate that sequential bound tightening (SBT)
significantly improves the efficiency and accuracy of Gurobi's SBnB algorithm.
Our results show that the proposed method can solve large-scale three-phase
infeasibility analysis problems with >5k nodes, achieving an optimality gap of
less than 10e-4. Furthermore, we demonstrate that by utilizing the developed
presolve routine for bounding, we can reduce the runtime of SBnB by up to 97%.

</details>


### [220] [Dynamic Switching Models for Truck-only Delivery and Drone-assisted Truck Delivery under Demand Uncertainty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16049)
*Jiaqing Lu,Qianwen Guo,Dian Sheng,Shumin Chen,Paul Schonfeld*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: Drones can improve truck delivery efficiency and reduce costs, especially in high-demand areas. This paper introduces a dynamic switching model to optimize the use of drones based on demand, showing significant cost savings compared to fixed strategies. The models are tested using data from Miami-Dade County.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Integrating drones into truck delivery systems can improve customer accessibility, reduce operational costs, and increase delivery efficiency. However, drone deployment incurs costs and its benefits depend on service demand, posing challenges in low-demand areas and due to uncertainties in demand prediction.

Method: A market entry and exit real option approach is used to optimize switching between truck-only and drone-assisted delivery under stochastic demand. A stochastic multiple-options model is developed to dynamically switch between truck-only and drone-assisted delivery with varying drone numbers.

Result: Deploying multiple drones per truck offers significant cost advantages in high-demand regions. The dynamic switching model reduces costs by 17.4% (deterministic) and 31.3% (stochastic) compared to immediate cost-saving switching. Sensitivity analysis reveals asymmetric effects of stochastic parameters on entry and exit timings.

Conclusion: Integrating drones into truck delivery systems offers significant cost advantages in high-demand regions, and dynamic switching models can reduce costs by up to 31.3% compared to immediate cost-saving switching. Sensitivity analysis shows asymmetric effects of stochastic parameters on entry and exit timings, and a stochastic multiple-options model allows for dynamic switching with varying drone numbers. The study provides valuable insights for optimizing logistics operations.

Abstract: Integrating drones into truck delivery systems can improve customer
accessibility, reduce operational costs, and increase delivery efficiency.
However, drone deployment incurs costs, including procurement, maintenance, and
energy consumption, and its benefits depend on service demand. In low-demand
areas, drone-assisted trucks may underutilize resources due to high upfront
costs. Accurately predicting demand is challenging due to uncertainties from
unforeseen events or infrastructure disruptions. To address this, a market
entry and exit real option approach is used to optimize switching between
truck-only and drone-assisted delivery under stochastic demand. Results show
that deploying multiple drones per truck offers significant cost advantages in
high-demand regions. Using the proposed dynamic switching model, deterministic
and stochastic approaches reduce costs by 17.4% and 31.3%, respectively,
compared to immediate cost-saving switching. Sensitivity analysis reveals
asymmetric effects of stochastic parameters on entry and exit timings. A
stochastic multiple-options model is further developed to dynamically switch
between truck-only and drone-assisted delivery with varying drone numbers.
Applying these models to Miami-Dade County, we evaluate dynamic switching costs
for three major logistics operators. This study highlights the potential
benefits of dynamic delivery switching and provides insights for optimizing
logistics operations.

</details>


### [221] [Data-Driven Analysis and Predictive Control of Descriptor Systems with Application to Power and Water Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16091)
*Yuan Zhang,Yu Wang,Jun Shang,Jinhui Zhang*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种数据驱动方法，用于分析和控制离散时间描述符系统，无需状态空间模型。研究解决了非因果性问题，提出了基于数据的可控性和可观性条件，并将Willems引理扩展到不完全可控系统。通过电网和供水网络的案例研究，证明了该方法在输出跟踪和保持性能方面的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管数据驱动分析和控制在工程领域日益受到关注，但对于包含代数约束（如电网和供水网络）的描述符系统而言，研究相对较少。因此，该研究旨在弥补这一空白，开发一种针对离散时间描述符系统的数据驱动分析和控制框架。

Method: 该研究提出了一种无需显式状态空间模型的数据驱动方法，通过构建前向和后向数据矩阵来处理非因果性问题，并提出了基于输入输出数据的可控性和可观性条件，同时将Willems引理扩展到不完全可控系统，最终实现了DeePC在描述符系统中的输出跟踪和在不完全可控条件下的性能保持。

Result: 该研究成功开发了一种数据驱动框架，用于分析和控制离散时间描述符系统。通过实例验证，该框架能够实现输出跟踪，并在频率调节（IEEE 9总线电网）和压力头控制（EPANET供水网络）的案例研究中，即使在R-可控性被违反的情况下，也能保持系统的稳定性和实现输出跟踪。

Conclusion: 该研究为离散时间描述符系统提供了一个全面的数据驱动框架，实现了在无需显式状态空间模型的情况下进行分析和控制，并成功应用于电网和供水网络的案例研究中。

Abstract: Despite growing interest in data-driven analysis and control of linear
systems, descriptor systems--which are essential for modeling complex
engineered systems with algebraic constraints like power and water
networks--have received comparatively little attention. This paper develops a
comprehensive data-driven framework for analyzing and controlling discrete-time
descriptor systems without relying on explicit state-space models. We address
fundamental challenges posed by non-causality through the construction of
forward and backward data matrices, establishing data-based sufficient
conditions for controllability and observability in terms of input-output data,
where both R-controllability and C-controllability (R-observability and
C-observability) have been considered. We then extend Willems' fundamental
lemma to incompletely controllable systems. These methodological advances
enable Data-Enabled Predictive Control (DeePC) to achieve output tracking in
descriptor systems and to maintain performance under incomplete controllability
conditions, as demonstrated in two case studies: i) Frequency regulation in an
IEEE 9-bus power system with 3 generators, where DeePC maintained the frequency
stability of the power system despite deliberate violations of
R-controllability; and ii) Pressure head control in an EPANET water network
with 3 tanks, 2 reservoirs, and 117 pipes, where output tracking was
successfully enforced under algebraic constraints.

### [222] [A Joint Delay-Energy-Security Aware Framework for Intelligent Task Scheduling in Satellite-Terrestrial Edge Computing Network](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16192)
*Yuhao Zheng,Ting You,Kejia Peng,Chang Liu*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 提出了一种用于卫星-陆地边缘计算网络（STECNs）的安全任务调度两阶段优化框架，通过用户关联和任务卸载平衡延迟、能耗和安全，并使用仿やや（MA）算法求解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为解决卫星-陆地边缘计算网络（STECNs）中安全任务调度的复杂性问题，需要一种能够联合考虑安全用户关联和任务卸载，并平衡传输延迟、能耗和物理层安全的优化框架。

Method: 提出了一种安全任务调度的两阶段优化框架，该框架联合考虑了安全用户关联和任务卸载，以平衡传输延迟、能耗和物理层安全。首先，通过离散化人工噪声（AN）功率比率和识别满足安全约束的可行链路，设计了一种感秘密的用户关联策略，从而产生一组候选安全关联。其次，将延迟-能量感知的任务调度问题公式化为整数线性规划，并使用启发式仿やや（MA）算法进行求解，以获得低复杂度、高质量的解决方案。

Result: 仿真结果证明了所提框架在实现安全高效任务调度方面的有效性和优越性。

Conclusion: 提出的框架在动态卫星环境中实现了安全高效的任务调度。

Abstract: In this paper, we propose a two-stage optimization framework for secure task
scheduling in satellite-terrestrial edge computing networks (STECNs). The
framework jointly considers secure user association and task offloading to
balance transmission delay, energy consumption, and physical-layer security. To
address the inherent complexity, we decouple the problem into two stages. In
the first stage, a secrecy-aware user association strategy is designed by
discretizing artificial noise (AN) power ratios and identifying feasible links
that satisfy secrecy constraints, resulting in a set of candidate secure
associations. In the second stage, we formulate a delay-energy-aware task
scheduling problem as an integer linear program and solve it using a heuristic
Mayfly Algorithm (MA) to obtain low-complexity, high-quality solutions.
Extensive simulation results demonstrate the effectiveness and superiority of
the proposed framework in achieving secure and efficient task scheduling under
dynamic satellite environments.

</details>


### [223] [Resilient Control for Networked Switched Systems With/Without ACK: An Active Quantized Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16296)
*Rui Zhao,Zhiqiang Zuo,Yijing Wang,Wentao Zhang,Yang Shi*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本研究提出了四种量化控制策略，用于在拒绝服务（DoS）攻击下的切换系统。这些策略考虑了不同的控制器、量化器和网络配置，并设计了更新律以避免饱和和保持一致性。通过推导稳定性条件，证明了所提出策略在DoS攻击下的有效性，并通过仿真进行了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 鉴于量化器和控制器的计算资源限制，以及系统防御能力，本研究旨在解决切换系统在拒绝服务（DoS）攻击下的量化控制问题。

Method: 本文针对具有拒绝服务（DoS）攻击的切换系统，设计了四种量化控制策略。这些策略结合了不同的控制器（有源和无源）、量化器（以原点为中心或定制设计）以及网络配置（带或不带确认信号）。为每种策略设计了特定的编码器和解码器更新律，以避免量化饱和，并通过传输额外信息来保持编码器和解码器操作的一致性。通过考虑异步行为，推导了关于切换信号和DoS攻击约束的充分条件，以实现渐近稳定性。此外，还提出了一种基于模型信息实时计算控制信号的有源量化策略，以及一种简化的无源量化策略，并研究了无确认信号的无源量化策略。

Result: 在拒绝服务（DoS）攻击下，所提出的有源量化策略（带确认信号）利用系统模型信息实时计算控制信号，实现了系统状态的收敛。一个精心设计的切换信号进一步缓解了DoS攻击的影响。一种简化的无源量化策略（带确认信号）也被开发出来，为无确认信号的策略奠定了基础。研究了无确认信号的无源量化策略，并提出了两种可行的量化器更新律。两次仿真验证了所提出策略的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了四种量化控制策略，并针对这些策略设计了特定的编码器和解码器更新律，以避免量化饱和并保持操作的统一性。通过考虑异步行为，推导了关于切换信号和拒绝服务（DoS）攻击约束的充分条件，以实现渐近稳定性。仿真结果验证了所提出策略的有效性。

Abstract: This paper deals with the quantized control problem for switched systems
under denial-of-service (DoS) attack.
  Considering the system's defensive capability and the computational resources
of quantizers and controllers, four control strategies are proposed. These
strategies incorporate different combinations of controllers (active and
passive), quantizers (centered on the origin or custom-designed), and network
configurations (with or without ACK signals). For each strategy, specific
update laws for the encoder and decoder are designed to avoid quantization
saturation.
  Furthermore, the uniformity of encoder and decoder operations is maintained
by transmitting additional information to the decoder. To achieve asymptotic
stability, sufficient conditions concerning the switching signal and DoS attack
constraints are derived by taking into account the asynchronous behaviors. The
proposed active quantization strategy with the ACK signal leverages the system
model information to compute the control signal in real-time, allowing for
possible convergence of the system state despite DoS attack. Additionally, a
well-designed switching signal is suggested to further mitigate the impact of
DoS attack. A passive quantization strategy with ACK signal is also developed
as a simplified version of the active quantized control strategy, providing the
foundation for a strategy without ACK signal. Inspired by time-triggered and
event-triggered mechanisms, the passive quantization strategy without ACK
signal is investigated, with two feasible update laws for the quantizer.
Finally, two simulations are conducted to validate the effectiveness of the
proposed strategies.

</details>

Abstract: This paper develops a new dynamic power profiling approach for modeling
AI-centric datacenter loads and analyzing their impact on grid operations,
particularly their potential to induce wide-area grid oscillations. We
characterize the periodic stochastic power fluctuations inherent to large-scale
AI workloads during both the training and fine-tuning stages, driven by the
state-of-the-art GPU computing architecture designs. These sustained, large
power fluctuations, unlike conventional load ramping, act as persistent forcing
inputs capable of interacting with and amplifying local and inter-area
oscillation modes. Using the WECC 179-bus system as a test case, we examine the
amplitude and variability of oscillatory responses under different factors,
ranging from system strength, penetration level, fluctuation frequency range,
individual datacenter size, to geographical deployment. Simulation results show
that, notably, narrower fluctuation bands, larger single-site capacities, or
dispersed siting can intensify oscillations across multiple modes. Our models
and numerical studies provide a quantitative basis for integrating AI-dominant
electricity demands into grid oscillation studies, and further support the
development of new planning and operational measures to power the continuous AI
load growth.

### [226] [Reinforcement Learning-based Control via Y-wise Affine Neural Networks (YANNs)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16474)
*Austin Braniff,Yuhe Tian*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于Y-wise Affine Neural Networks (YANNs) 的强化学习（RL）算法（YANN-RL）。该算法利用YANNs的可解释性和精确表示能力，初始化RL的actor和critic网络，使其能够从线性最优控制的置信度开始。通过增加额外的网络层来处理非线性表达式，YANN-RL能够在线学习并最终解决复杂的非线性最优控制问题。实验结果表明，YANN-RL在处理安全约束方面表现优于DDPG算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: YANNs提供了一种可解释的神经网络，可以精确表示在任意数量的等 संभाव子域上定义的任意输入和输出维度的分段仿射函数。YANNs的一个代表性应用是重新表述多参数线性模型预测控制的显式解。在此基础上，提出使用YANNs初始化RL actor和critic网络，使生成的YANN-RL控制算法能够从线性最优控制的置信度开始。

Method: 提出了一种基于Y-wise Affine Neural Networks (YANNs) 的新型强化学习（RL）算法。YANNs提供了一种可解释的神经网络，可以精确表示在任意数量的等 संभाव子域上定义的任意输入和输出维度的分段仿射函数。YANNs的一个代表性应用是重新表述多参数线性模型预测控制的显式解。在此基础上，提出使用YANNs初始化RL actor和critic网络，使生成的YANN-RL控制算法能够从线性最优控制的置信度开始。YANN-actor通过表示通过使用近似线性系统模型的离线计算获得的控制解来初始化。YANN-critic表示状态-动作价值函数对于线性系统以及作为最优控制问题（OCP）目标的对象函数的显式形式。通过注入额外的网络层来扩展YANNs以处理非线性表达式，这些表达式可以通过与真实的复杂非线性系统进行在线交互来训练。通过这种方式，策略和状态价值函数最初都可以精确地表示线性OCP，并最终能够学习通用非线性OCP的解。还实现了连续策略改进，以提供线性OCP解作为RL策略性能的有效下界的启发式置信度。

Result: YANN-RL算法在剪辑的摆锤和安全关键的化学反应系统中得到了验证。结果表明，YANN-RL在考虑安全约束时，其性能显著优于使用深度确定性策略梯度（DDPG）的现代强化学习算法。

Conclusion: YANN-RL算法在剪辑的摆锤和安全关键的化学反应系统中得到了验证，结果表明YANN-RL显著优于使用深度确定性策略梯度（DDPG）的现代强化学习算法，尤其是在考虑安全约束方面。

Abstract: This work presents a novel reinforcement learning (RL) algorithm based on
Y-wise Affine Neural Networks (YANNs). YANNs provide an interpretable neural
network which can exactly represent known piecewise affine functions of
arbitrary input and output dimensions defined on any amount of polytopic
subdomains. One representative application of YANNs is to reformulate explicit
solutions of multi-parametric linear model predictive control. Built on this,
we propose the use of YANNs to initialize RL actor and critic networks, which
enables the resulting YANN-RL control algorithm to start with the confidence of
linear optimal control. The YANN-actor is initialized by representing the
multi-parametric control solutions obtained via offline computation using an
approximated linear system model. The YANN-critic represents the explicit form
of the state-action value function for the linear system and the reward
function as the objective in an optimal control problem (OCP). Additional
network layers are injected to extend YANNs for nonlinear expressions, which
can be trained online by directly interacting with the true complex nonlinear
system. In this way, both the policy and state-value functions exactly
represent a linear OCP initially and are able to eventually learn the solution
of a general nonlinear OCP. Continuous policy improvement is also implemented
to provide heuristic confidence that the linear OCP solution serves as an
effective lower bound to the performance of RL policy. The YANN-RL algorithm is
demonstrated on a clipped pendulum and a safety-critical chemical-reactive
system. Our results show that YANN-RL significantly outperforms the modern RL
algorithm using deep deterministic policy gradient, especially when considering
safety constraints.

</details>


### [227] [Multi-agent Robust and Optimal Policy Learning for Data Harvesting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16490)
*Shili Wu,Yancheng Zhu,Aniruddha Datta,Sean B. Andersson*

TL;DR: Error

Motivation: Error

Method: Error

Result: Error

Conclusion: Error

Abstract: We consider the problem of using multiple agents to harvest data from a
collection of sensor nodes (targets) scattered across a two-dimensional
environment. These targets transmit their data to the agents that move in the
space above them, and our goal is for the agents to collect data from the
targets as efficiently as possible while moving to their final destinations.
The agents are assumed to have a continuous control action, and we leverage
reinforcement learning, specifically Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) with
Lagrangian Penalty (LP), to identify highly effective solutions. Additionally,
we enhance the controller's robustness by incorporating regularization at each
state to smooth the learned policy. We conduct a series of simulations to
demonstrate our approach and validate its performance and robustness.

### [228] [Spike Agreement Dependent Plasticity: A scalable Bio-Inspired learning paradigm for Spiking Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2508.16216)
*Saptarshi Bej,Muhammed Sahad E,Gouri Lakshmi,Harshit Kumar,Pritam Kar,Bikas C Das*

Main category: cs.NE

TL;DR: SADP 是一种新的 SNN 学习规则，它基于脉冲序列的一致性而不是精确的时序，通过位逻辑实现线性时间复杂度，并在 MNIST 和 Fashion-MNIST 上提供了比 STDP 更好的准确性和运行时间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受生物启发的突触学习规则通常在生物保真度和计算效率之间存在权衡。本文旨在弥合生物保真度和计算可扩展性之间的差距。

Method: SADP 是一种受生物启发的突触学习规则，它不依赖于精确的脉冲-脉冲配对时序，而是依赖于前馈和后馈脉冲序列之间的一致性。SADP 通过用群体相关性指标（如 Cohen's kappa）替换脉冲-脉冲配对时序更新，来泛化经典的 STDP。SADP 更新规则具有线性时间复杂度，并支持通过位逻辑进行高效的硬件实现。

Result: 在 MNIST 和 Fashion-MNIST 上的实验结果表明，SADP（特别是当配备从我们的实验性离子电有机记忆晶体管设备数据派生出的基于样条的核时）在准确性和运行时间方面均优于经典的 STDP。

Conclusion: SADP 是一种受生物启发的、适用于脉冲神经网络 (SNN) 的突触学习规则，它通过对群体发放相关性指标（如 Cohen's kappa）的依赖，并能线性实现，因此在准确性和运行时间方面均优于经典的 STDP，为神经形态系统提供了一种可行的学习机制。

Abstract: We introduce Spike Agreement Dependent Plasticity (SADP), a biologically
inspired synaptic learning rule for Spiking Neural Networks (SNNs) that relies
on the agreement between pre- and post-synaptic spike trains rather than
precise spike-pair timing. SADP generalizes classical Spike-Timing-Dependent
Plasticity (STDP) by replacing pairwise temporal updates with population-level
correlation metrics such as Cohen's kappa. The SADP update rule admits
linear-time complexity and supports efficient hardware implementation via
bitwise logic. Empirical results on MNIST and Fashion-MNIST show that SADP,
especially when equipped with spline-based kernels derived from our
experimental iontronic organic memtransistor device data, outperforms classical
STDP in both accuracy and runtime. Our framework bridges the gap between
biological plausibility and computational scalability, offering a viable
learning mechanism for neuromorphic systems.
